<ol><li>impassable

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> utter, rank, hopeless

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непьющий.html>непью́щий</a> (14009)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пью́щий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pʹjúščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непьющий.html>непью́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nepʹjúščij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>non-drinking, abstinent, teetotaling</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неравнодушный.html>неравноду́шный</a> (17794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неравнодушный.html>неравноду́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neravnodúšnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(of a person, or an attitude or approach) caring, not indifferent</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неразбериха.html>неразбери́ха</a> (13918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разбер-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razber-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sort out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, using the present-tense stem of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разобраться.html>разобра́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razobrátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; literally "thing that can't be sorted out".

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неразборчивый.html>неразбо́рчивый</a> (8919)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разборчивый.html>разбо́рчивый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbórčivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неразборчивый.html>неразбо́рчивый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerazbórčivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>illegible, indecipherable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неразборчивый.html>неразбо́рчивый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>по́черк</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nerazbórčivyj</b> póčerk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">indecipherable handwriting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>inarticulate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неразборчивый.html>неразбо́рчивые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nerazbórčivyje</b> slová</i> ― <span class="e-translation">inarticulate words</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>undemanding, undiscerning
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неразборчивый.html>неразбо́рчивый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вкус.html>вкус</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nerazbórčivyj</b> vkus</i> ― <span class="e-translation">undiscerning taste</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>unscrupulous, unprincipled</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разреши́мый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrešímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нервировать.html>нерви́ровать</a> (24996)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нервировать.html>нерви́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nervírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nerve; nervous

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нервный.html>не́рвная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nérvnaja sistéma</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>nervous</b> system</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>nervous, easily excitable or provoked
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотрудник.html>сотру́дник</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оказаться.html>оказа́лся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нервный.html>не́рвным</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молоды́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:парень.html>па́рнем</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nóvyj sotrúdnik okazálsja <b>nérvnym</b> molodým párnem.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The new employee was a <b>nervous</b> young man.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>nerve-wracking, creating a lot of worry
